 /* Hent ægtefælle på csrp                                            */
 /*********************************************************************/
 Check_CSRP: proc;                                                      
                                                                        
          CSRP_FUNDET = NEJ;                                            
                                                                        
          EXEC SQL                                                      
            SELECT                                                      
               pnr,                                                     
               AEGTFPNR,                                                
               civiskod,                                                
               cvisfradto                                               
                                                                        
            INTO                                                        
               :DCLBQ70000T.PNR,                                        
               :DCLBQ70000T.AEGTFPNR,                                   
               :DCLBQ70000T.CIVISKOD,                                   
               :DCLBQ70000T.CVISFRADTO                                  
            FROM BQ70000T                                               
            WHERE pnr   = :WS_CSRP_PNR;                                 
                                                                        
         SELECT(SQLCA.SQLCODE);                                         
            WHEN(0) DO;                                                 
               CSRP_FUNDET = JA;                                        
            END;                                                        
            WHEN(100) DO;                                               
            END;                                                        
            OTHERWISE DO;                                               
               ABENDTXT = '101 SELECT BQ70000T';                        
               CALL SQL_FEJL;                                           
            END;                                                        
         END;                                                           
                                                                        
 END Check_CSRP;                                                        
 /*********************************************************************/
 /* QEB TILFØJET 18-01-2018 TIL AT FINDE SLUT OPLYSNING SOM SKAL      */
 /* SLETTES FRA BQ77000T FORDI DER BLEVET KOPIERET FRA GENERATION 1   */
 /* TIL ET HØJRE GENERATIONS NUMMER                                   */
 /*********************************************************************/
 /*********************************************************************/
 /* UNDERSØG OM DER FINDES GENRATION 2 ELLER MERE I ESR TABELLER      */
 /*********************************************************************/
 SELECT_ESR_MED_GEN2_ELLER_MERE: PROC;                                  
                                                                        
         IF TEST_PUT                                                    
         THEN DO;                                                       
            PUT SKIP LIST('SELECT_ESR_MED_GEN2_ELLER_MERE');            
            PUT SKIP LIST('DCLBQ77000T.DCPRN =',DCLBQ77000T.DCPRN);     
            PUT SKIP LIST('DCLBQ77000T.EKOMNR=',DCLBQ77000T.EKOMNR);    
            PUT SKIP LIST('DCLBQ77000T.EEJDNR=',DCLBQ77000T.EEJDNR);    
         END;                                                           
                                                                        
         ESR_MED_HØJRE_GEN_FUNDET = NEJ;                                
                                                                        
         EXEC SQL                                                       
            SELECT                                                      
               TIL_EVS_AAR,                                             
               AFVIKLINGS_ID,                                           
               DCPRCIR,                                                 
               EKOMNR,                                                  
               EEJDNR,                                                  
               EGENNR                                                   
            INTO                                                        
              :DCLBQ75000T.TIL_EVS_AAR,                                 
              :DCLBQ75000T.AFVIKLINGS_ID,                               
              :DCLBQ75000T.DCPRCIR,                                     
              :DCLBQ75000T.EKOMNR,                                      
              :DCLBQ75000T.EEJDNR,                                      
              :DCLBQ75000T.EGENNR                                       
                                                                        
           FROM BQ75000T                                                
           WHERE TIL_EVS_AAR   = :WS_TIL_EVS_AAR                        
            AND  AFVIKLINGS_ID = :WS_FORSKUD_SLUT_TXT                   
            AND  DCPRCIR       = :DCLBQ77000T.DCPRN                     
            AND  EKOMNR        = :DCLBQ77000T.EKOMNR                    
            AND  EEJDNR        = :DCLBQ77000T.EEJDNR                    
            AND  EGENNR        > 1                                      
          FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY;                                       
                                                                        
                                                                        
         SELECT(SQLCA.SQLCODE);                                         
            WHEN(0) DO;                                                 
               ESR_MED_HØJRE_GEN_FUNDET = '1'B;                         
            END;                                                        
            WHEN(100) DO;                                               
            END;                                                        
            OTHERWISE DO;                                               
               FEJLTEKST = 'SELECT GEN2+ BQ75000T GÅET GALT';           
               CALL SQL_FEJL;                                           
            END;                                                        
         END;                                                           
                                                                        
 END SELECT_ESR_MED_GEN2_ELLER_MERE;                                    
 /*********************************************************************/
 DELETE_GEN1_BQ77000T: PROC;                                            
                                                                        
       IF TEST_PUT                                                      
       THEN DO;                                                         
          PUT SKIP LIST('DELETE_GEN1_BQ77000T');                        
          PUT SKIP LIST('DCLBQ77000T.DCPRN =',DCLBQ77000T.DCPRN);       
          PUT SKIP LIST('DCLBQ77000T.EKOMNR=',DCLBQ77000T.EKOMNR);      
          PUT SKIP LIST('DCLBQ77000T.EEJDNR=',DCLBQ77000T.EEJDNR);      
       END;                                                             
                                                                        
       EXEC SQL DELETE                                                  
       FROM BQ77000T T77                                                
       WHERE T77.TIL_EVS_AAR    = :WS_TIL_EVS_AAR                       
         AND T77.AFVIKLINGS_ID  = :WS_FORSKUD_SLUT_TXT                  
         AND T77.DCPRN          = :DCLBQ77000T.DCPRN                    
         AND T77.EKOMNR         = :DCLBQ77000T.EKOMNR                   
         AND T77.EEJDNR         = :DCLBQ77000T.EEJDNR                   
         AND T77.EGENNR         = 1;                                    
                                                                        
       SELECT (SQLCA.SQLCODE);                                          
         WHEN (0)                                                       
           DO;                                                          
             IF TEST_PUT                                                
             THEN DO;                                                   
                PUT SKIP LIST('DELETE_GEN1_BQ77000T OK');               
             END;                                                       
             EXEC SQL COMMIT;                                           
           END;                                                         
         OTHERWISE                                                      
           DO;                                                          
            FEJLTEKST  =  'DELETE GEN1 BQ77000T';                       
            CALL SQL_FEJL;                                              
           END;                                                         
       END; /* SELECT*/                                                 
                                                                        
                                                                        
 END DELETE_GEN1_BQ77000T;                                              
 /*********************************************************************/
 END  BH80100;
